ceiling.\n- Set the overall size of the classroom to comfortably fit 20 student desks and chairs arranged in 4 rows of 5 desks each. Leave clear aisles between rows and columns.\n- Create 20 student desks as rectangular tables positioned on the floor, each with a corresponding chair facing the front of the classroom.\n- Add a large teacher\'s desk centered at the front of the room, facing the student desks, with a matching chair behind it.\n- Place a large rectangular blackboard on the front wall above the teacher\'s desk.\n- Install a ceiling-mounted projector aligned with the blackboard position.\n- Position a tall bookshelf filled with books along the right side wall.\n- Attach a circular wall clock on the left side wall, visible from all desks.\n- Place a potted plant in the back-left corner of the room for decoration.\n- Install evenly spaced bright ceiling lights across the classroom.\n- Put educational posters or charts evenly spaced on the left and right walls.\n- Add a large window with curtains located on the back wall, centered.\n- Place two waste bins: one near the teacher\'s desk and one at
